Similarly to the book, we can introduce equational reasoning in agda.
I'm using the definitions from the [agda-stdlib](https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2708).

## Section 2.4 Homotopies and equivalences

<a id="11378" class="Comment">-- Theorem 2.6.4.</a>

## 2.7 Σ-types

I'm using a slightly different definition of the `f` in the following
theorem, as it'll be useful further on.

## 2.9 Π-types and the function extensionality axiom

<pre class="Agda"><a id="happly"></a><a id="14110" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14110" class="Function">happly</a> <a id="14117" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14119" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14120" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14120" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14124" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="14126" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="14127" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14129" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14130" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14130" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14132" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14134" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14120" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14136" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14138" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="14140" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="14141" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14143" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14144" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14144" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14146" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14146" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14148" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14150" href="Chapter1.Book.html#743" class="Function">Π</a> <a id="14152" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14130" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14153" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="14162" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14164" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14144" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14166" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3971" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="14168" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14146" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14170" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14172" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14144" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14174" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5694" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="14176" href="Chapter2.Book.html#14146" class="Bound">g</a>

## 2.10 Universes and the univalence axiom

## 2.11 Identity type

<pre class="Agda"><a id="20536" class="Comment">-- Lemma 2.11.2.</a>
<a id="isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap"></a><a id="20553" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20553" class="Function">isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap</a> <a id="20572" class="Symbol">:</a>
             <a id="20587" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20588" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20588" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20592" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="20594" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="20595" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20598" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20598" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20602" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="20604" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="20605" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="20618" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20621" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20621" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20625" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20588" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20629" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20598" class="Bound">B</a><a id="20630" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="20643" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20645" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7440" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="20653" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20621" class="Bound">f</a>

## Additional commentaries

    <a id="32610" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32610" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="32616" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32619" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32619" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="32621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32623" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32479" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32625" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3971" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="32627" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32481" class="Bound">B</a><a id="32628" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32630" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32633" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32479" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32635" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32637" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8705" class="Function">≃-refl</a> <a id="32644" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32479" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32645" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32647" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3971" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="32649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32650" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32481" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32652" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32654" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8217" class="Function">≃-→</a> <a id="32658" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32659" href="Chapter2.Book.html#16147" class="Function">≡-𝒰-≃</a> <a id="32665" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32479" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32667" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32481" class="Bound">B</a><a id="32668" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32670" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32619" class="Bound">p</a><a id="32671" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="32677" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32610" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="32683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32684" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3931" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="32689" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32689" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32690" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32692" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32694" href="Chapter2.Book.html#12164" class="Function">pair⁼</a><a id="32699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32700" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3931" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="32705" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="32707" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32709" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3931" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="32714" class="Symbol">_)</a>
</pre>
Also `×` is commutative in the following sense
<pre class="Agda"><a id="×-comm"></a><a id="32777" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32777" class="Function">×-comm</a> <a id="32784" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32787" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32787" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32789" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32791" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="32793" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="32794" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32796" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32797" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32797" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32799" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32801" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="32803" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="32804" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32806" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32808" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32787" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32810" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1653" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="32812" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32797" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32814" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8100" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="32816" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32797" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32818" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1653" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="32820" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32787" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="32822" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32777" class="Function">×-comm</a> <a id="32829" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32829" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32831" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32831" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="32833" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32835" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32882" class="Function">map</a> <a id="32839" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32841" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7612" class="Function">invs⇒equivs</a> <a id="32853" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32882" class="Function">map</a> <a id="32857" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32858" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32910" class="Function">map⁻¹</a> <a id="32864" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32866" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32940" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="32868" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32870" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32951" class="Function">η</a><a id="32871" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="32874" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="32882" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32882" class="Function">map</a> <a id="32886" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="32888" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="32890" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32891" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32891" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="32893" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32895" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32895" class="Bound">y</a><a id="32896" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32898" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32901" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32895" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="32903" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="32905" href="Chapter2.Book.html#32891" class="Bound">x</a><a id="32906" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="33096" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33099" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33101" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33101" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33103" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33105" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33053" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33107" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33109" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33063" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33111" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33101" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33113" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1653" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33115" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33077" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="33116" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33118" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8100" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="33120" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="33122" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33124" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33124" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33126" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33128" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33053" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33130" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33132" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33063" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33134" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33124" class="Bound">x</a><a id="33135" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33137" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1653" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33139" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33077" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="33140" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="33199" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="33207" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33207" class="Function">map</a> <a id="33211" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33213" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="33215" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33216" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33216" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33218" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33220" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33220" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33222" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33224" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33224" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33225" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33227" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33229" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="33231" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33216" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33233" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33235" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33220" class="Bound">y</a><a id="33236" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33238" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33240" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33224" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33241" class="Symbol">)</a>

`Σ` commutes with itself in the sense that
<pre class="Agda"><a id="Σ-comm"></a><a id="33361" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33361" class="Function">Σ-comm</a> <a id="33368" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33371" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33371" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33375" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="33377" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="33378" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33380" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33381" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33381" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33385" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="33387" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="33388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33391" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33391" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33395" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33371" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33399" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33381" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33403" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="33405" href="Chapter1.Book.html#332" class="Generalizable">𝓀</a><a id="33406" class="Symbol">)</a>
       <a id="33415" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33418" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33420" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33420" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33422" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33424" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33371" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33426" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33428" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33430" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33430" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33432" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33434" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33381" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33436" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33438" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33391" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33440" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33420" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33442" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33430" class="Bound">y</a><a id="33443" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33445" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8100" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="33447" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33448" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33450" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33450" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33452" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33454" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33381" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33456" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33458" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="33460" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33460" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33462" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="33464" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33371" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33466" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1548" class="Function">,</a> <a id="33468" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33391" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33470" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33460" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33472" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33450" class="Bound">y</a><a id="33473" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="33475" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33361" class="Function">Σ-comm</a> <a id="33482" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33482" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="33484" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33486" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33533" class="Function">map</a> <a id="33490" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33492" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7612" class="Function">invs⇒equivs</a> <a id="33504" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33533" class="Function">map</a> <a id="33508" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33509" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33569" class="Function">map⁻¹</a> <a id="33515" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33517" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33607" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="33519" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33521" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33618" class="Function">η</a><a id="33522" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="33525" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="33533" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33533" class="Function">map</a> <a id="33537" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33539" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="33541" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33542" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33542" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33544" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33546" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33546" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33548" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33550" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33550" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33551" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33553" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33556" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33546" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33558" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33560" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33542" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33562" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33564" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33550" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33565" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="33569" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33569" class="Function">map⁻¹</a> <a id="33575" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33577" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="33579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33580" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33580" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33582" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33584" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33584" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33586" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33588" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33588" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33589" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33591" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33594" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33584" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33596" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33598" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33580" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="33600" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1499" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33602" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33588" class="Bound">z</a><a id="33603" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="33607" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33607" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="33609" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33611" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3931" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="33618" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33618" class="Function">η</a> <a id="33620" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33622" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3931" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
Since we don't have cumulativity we'll use the fact that `raise` is a equivalence.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="raise⁻¹"></a><a id="33724" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33724" class="Function">raise⁻¹</a> <a id="33732" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33735" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33735" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="33737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33739" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="33744" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33747" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33749" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33751" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="33753" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="33754" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33756" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33758" href="Chapter1.Book.html#617" class="Datatype">Raised</a> <a id="33765" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33735" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="33767" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33769" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33771" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33747" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="33773" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33724" class="Function">raise⁻¹</a> <a id="33781" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33781" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="33783" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33783" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33785" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33786" href="Chapter1.Book.html#666" class="InductiveConstructor">raise</a> <a id="33792" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33792" class="Bound">x</a><a id="33793" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33795" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33797" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33792" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="≡-Raised-≃"></a><a id="33800" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33800" class="Function">≡-Raised-≃</a> <a id="33811" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33813" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33814" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33814" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="33816" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33818" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="33823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33826" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33826" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33830" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="33832" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="33833" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33835" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33837" href="Chapter1.Book.html#617" class="Datatype">Raised</a> <a id="33844" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33814" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="33846" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33826" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33848" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8100" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="33850" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33826" class="Bound">A</a>
